--- Views/Sellers/Index.cshtml ---

@model ThriftLoop.ViewModels.SellersViewModel
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.ViewModels
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@using System.Text.Json
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Sellers";
    Layout = null;

    var categories = ItemCreateViewModel.Categories;
    var conditions = ItemCreateViewModel.Conditions;
    var maxPrice = Model.Items.Any()
        ? (int)Math.Ceiling((double)Model.Items.Max(i => i.Price))
        : 100000;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Sellers.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />
</head>
<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")

    <div class="container">
        <div class="fy-shell">

            @* ── Left: filter sidebar (mirrors Home) ─────────────────────────────── *@
            <aside class="fy-sidebar" id="fySidebar" aria-label="Filter listings">

                <div class="fy-sidebar__header">
                    <span class="fy-sidebar__title">Filters</span>
                    <button type="button" class="fy-sidebar__reset" id="resetFilters">Clear all</button>
                </div>

                <div class="fy-filter-group">
                    <label class="fy-filter-group__label" for="searchInput">Search</label>
                    <div class="fy-search-wrap">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor"
                             stroke-width="1.6" aria-hidden="true">
                            <circle cx="8.5" cy="8.5" r="5.5" />
                            <path d="M13.5 13.5L18 18" stroke-linecap="round" />
                        </svg>
                        <input type="search" id="searchInput" class="fy-search-input"
                               placeholder="Title, description or shop…" autocomplete="off" />
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="fy-filter-group">
                    <label class="fy-filter-group__label">Price</label>
                    <div class="fy-price-row">
                        <div class="fy-price-field">
                            <span class="fy-price-field__sym">₱</span>
                            <input type="number" id="priceMin" class="fy-price-input"
                                   placeholder="0" min="0" max="@maxPrice" value="0" />
                        </div>
                        <span class="fy-price-sep">–</span>
                        <div class="fy-price-field">
                            <span class="fy-price-field__sym">₱</span>
                            <input type="number" id="priceMax" class="fy-price-input"
                                   placeholder="@maxPrice" min="0" max="@maxPrice" value="@maxPrice" />
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="fy-filter-group">
                    <p class="fy-filter-group__label">Category</p>
                    <ul class="fy-check-list" id="catFilters">
                        @foreach (var cat in categories)
                        {
                            <li>
                                <label class="fy-check-label">
                                    <input type="checkbox" class="fy-check" value="@cat" />
                                    <span class="fy-check-box"></span>
                                    <span class="fy-check-text">@cat</span>
                                </label>
                            </li>
                        }
                    </ul>
                </div>

                <div class="fy-filter-group">
                    <p class="fy-filter-group__label">Condition</p>
                    <ul class="fy-check-list" id="condFilters">
                        @foreach (var cond in conditions)
                        {
                            <li>
                                <label class="fy-check-label">
                                    <input type="checkbox" class="fy-check" value="@cond" />
                                    <span class="fy-check-box"></span>
                                    <span class="fy-check-text">@cond</span>
                                </label>
                            </li>
                        }
                    </ul>
                </div>

            </aside>

            @* ── Right: feed ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
            <main class="fy-main" id="fyMain">

                <header class="fy-feed-header">
                    <h1 class="fy-feed-title">Sellers</h1>
                    <p class="fy-feed-meta" id="feedMeta">
                        <span id="visibleCount">@Model.Items.Count</span>&nbsp;listings
                    </p>
                </header>

                @* ── Shop suggestion row ──────────────────────────────────────────── *@
                @if (Model.Shops.Any())
                {
                    <div class="sl-shops-section">
                        <p class="sl-shops-section__label">Shops</p>
                        <div class="sl-shops-row" id="shopsRow">
                            @foreach (var shop in Model.Shops)
                            {
                                <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Index"
                                   asp-route-id="@shop.Id"
                                   class="sl-shop-card"
                                   data-shop-name="@shop.ShopName.ToLower()">

                                    @* Logo *@
                                    @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(shop.LogoUrl))
                                    {
                                        <img src="@shop.LogoUrl" alt="@shop.ShopName"
                                             class="sl-shop-card__logo" loading="lazy" />
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        <div class="sl-shop-card__logo sl-shop-card__logo--placeholder"
                                             aria-hidden="true">
                                            @char.ToUpper(shop.ShopName.FirstOrDefault())
                                        </div>
                                    }

                                    <span class="sl-shop-card__name">@shop.ShopName</span>

                                    @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(shop.Bio))
                                    {
                                        <span class="sl-shop-card__bio">@shop.Bio</span>
                                    }

                                </a>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }

                @* ── Items feed ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
                @if (!Model.Items.Any())
                {
                    <div class="fy-empty" id="globalEmpty">
                        <div class="fy-empty__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                <rect x="8" y="14" width="48" height="36" rx="6" />
                                <path d="M22 14v-4a6 6 0 0112 0v4" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                <path d="M24 33h16M32 25v16" stroke-linecap="round" />
                            </svg>
                        </div>
                        <h2 class="fy-empty__title">No shop listings yet</h2>
                        <p class="fy-empty__body">Sellers haven't posted any items.</p>
                    </div>
                }
                else
                {
                    <div class="fy-empty fy-empty--hidden" id="filterEmpty" aria-live="polite">
                        <div class="fy-empty__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                <circle cx="28" cy="28" r="18" />
                                <path d="M42 42l14 14" stroke-linecap="round" />
                                <path d="M22 28h12M28 22v12" stroke-linecap="round" />
                            </svg>
                        </div>
                        <h2 class="fy-empty__title">No matches</h2>
                        <p class="fy-empty__body">Try adjusting or clearing your filters.</p>
                        <button type="button" class="fy-empty__reset-btn" id="resetFilters2">
                            Clear filters
                        </button>
                    </div>

                    <div class="fy-grid" id="itemGrid">
                        @foreach (var item in Model.Items)
                        {
                            var isOwner = Model.CurrentUserId.HasValue
                            && item.UserId == Model.CurrentUserId.Value;
                            var imagesJson = JsonSerializer.Serialize(item.ImageUrls);

                            @* Resolve shop name for search / display *@
                            var shopName = item.Shop?.ShopName ?? string.Empty;

                            <article class="fy-card fy-card--shop"
                                     data-category="@item.Category"
                                     data-condition="@item.Condition"
                                     data-price="@item.Price.ToString("F2", System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)"
                                     data-title="@item.Title.ToLower()"
                                     data-desc="@item.Description.ToLower()"
                                     data-shop="@shopName.ToLower()">

                                <div class="fy-card__img-wrap" data-images="@imagesJson">

                                    @if (item.ImageUrls.Count > 0)
                                    {
                                        <img src="@item.ImageUrls[0]" alt="@item.Title"
                                             class="fy-card__img" loading="lazy" />

                                        @if (item.ImageUrls.Count > 1)
                                        {
                                            <div class="fy-card__dots" aria-hidden="true">
                                                @for (int d = 0; d < item.ImageUrls.Count; d++)
                                                {
                                                    <span class="fy-card__dot @(d == 0 ? "fy-card__dot--active" : "")"></span>
                                                }
                                            </div>
                                        }
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        <div class="fy-card__img fy-card__img--placeholder" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <svg viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                                <rect x="4" y="8" width="40" height="32" rx="4" />
                                                <circle cx="17" cy="20" r="4" />
                                                <path d="M4 36l12-10 8 8 6-5 14 11"
                                                      stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                            </svg>
                                        </div>
                                    }

                                    <span class="fy-card__condition-badge">@item.Condition</span>
                                    <span class="fy-card__shop-badge" aria-label="Shop listing">Shop</span>

                                    @if (isOwner)
                                    {
                                        <span class="fy-card__owner-badge" aria-label="Your listing">
                                            Your listing
                                        </span>
                                    }
                                </div>

                                <div class="fy-card__body">
                                    <div class="fy-card__top">
                                        <span class="fy-card__category">@item.Category</span>
                                        <span class="fy-card__date">@item.CreatedAt.ToString("MMM d")</span>
                                    </div>

                                    @* Price display section in the card body *@
                                    <h2 class="fy-card__title">@item.Title</h2>

                                    <p class="fy-card__price">
                                        @if (Model.ShopItemPriceDisplay.ContainsKey(item.Id))
                                        {
                                            @Model.ShopItemPriceDisplay[item.Id]
                                        }
                                        else
                                        {
                                            <span>₱@item.Price.ToString("N2")</span>
                                        }
                                    </p>

                                    @* Shop attribution line *@
                                    @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(shopName))
                                    {
                                        <p class="fy-card__shop-attr">@shopName</p>
                                    }

                                    <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Details"
                                       asp-route-id="@item.Id"
                                       class="fy-card__link"
                                       aria-label="View details for @item.Title">
                                    </a>
                                </div>

                                @if (isOwner)
                                {
                                    <div class="fy-card__actions fy-card__actions--owner">
                                        <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Edit"
                                           asp-route-id="@item.Id"
                                           class="fy-btn fy-btn--manage">
                                            Manage listing
                                        </a>
                                    </div>
                                }

                            </article>
                        }
                    </div>
                }

            </main>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var grid         = document.getElementById('itemGrid');
            var shopsRow     = document.getElementById('shopsRow');
            var filterEmpty  = document.getElementById('filterEmpty');
            var visibleCount = document.getElementById('visibleCount');
            var searchInput  = document.getElementById('searchInput');
            var priceMin     = document.getElementById('priceMin');
            var priceMax     = document.getElementById('priceMax');
            var catChecks    = document.querySelectorAll('#catFilters .fy-check');
            var condChecks   = document.querySelectorAll('#condFilters .fy-check');

            var cards     = grid     ? Array.prototype.slice.call(grid.querySelectorAll('.fy-card'))          : [];
            var shopCards = shopsRow ? Array.prototype.slice.call(shopsRow.querySelectorAll('.sl-shop-card')) : [];

            // ── Multi-image hover cycling ─────────────────────────────────────
            cards.forEach(function (card) {
                var wrap   = card.querySelector('.fy-card__img-wrap');
                var img    = card.querySelector('.fy-card__img');
                var dotsEl = card.querySelector('.fy-card__dots');
                if (!wrap || !img) return;

                var images = [];
                try { images = JSON.parse(wrap.getAttribute('data-images') || '[]'); } catch(e) {}
                if (images.length < 2) return;

                var dots    = dotsEl ? Array.prototype.slice.call(dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.fy-card__dot')) : [];
                var current = 0;
                var timer   = null;

                function goTo(idx) {
                    img.classList.add('fy-img--fading');
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        img.src = images[idx];
                        img.classList.remove('fy-img--fading');
                    }, 220);
                    dots.forEach(function (d, i) { d.classList.toggle('fy-card__dot--active', i === idx); });
                    current = idx;
                }

                card.addEventListener('mouseenter', function () {
                    if (timer) return;
                    timer = setInterval(function () { goTo((current + 1) % images.length); }, 900);
                });
                card.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {
                    if (timer) { clearInterval(timer); timer = null; }
                    if (current !== 0) goTo(0);
                });
            });

            // ── Filter ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function applyFilters() {
                var query  = searchInput ? searchInput.value.trim().toLowerCase() : '';
                var minVal = priceMin    ? parseFloat(priceMin.value) || 0        : 0;
                var maxVal = priceMax    ? parseFloat(priceMax.value) || Infinity : Infinity;

                var activeCats  = [];
                var activeConds = [];
                catChecks.forEach(function (cb)  { if (cb.checked) activeCats.push(cb.value); });
                condChecks.forEach(function (cb) { if (cb.checked) activeConds.push(cb.value); });

                var shown = 0;

                cards.forEach(function (card) {
                    var price = parseFloat(card.dataset.price);
                    var catOk   = activeCats.length  === 0 || activeCats.indexOf(card.dataset.category)  !== -1;
                    var condOk  = activeConds.length === 0 || activeConds.indexOf(card.dataset.condition) !== -1;
                    var priceOk = price >= minVal && price <= maxVal;
                    var textOk  = !query
                        || (card.dataset.title  || '').indexOf(query) !== -1
                        || (card.dataset.desc   || '').indexOf(query) !== -1
                        || (card.dataset.shop   || '').indexOf(query) !== -1;

                    var visible = catOk && condOk && priceOk && textOk;
                    card.classList.toggle('fy-card--hidden', !visible);
                    if (visible) shown++;
                });

                // Also filter shop cards in the suggestion row by search text
                shopCards.forEach(function (sc) {
                    var name = sc.dataset.shopName || '';
                    sc.classList.toggle('sl-shop-card--hidden',
                        query.length > 0 && name.indexOf(query) === -1);
                });

                if (visibleCount) visibleCount.textContent = shown;
                if (filterEmpty)  filterEmpty.classList.toggle('fy-empty--hidden', shown > 0);
            }

            if (searchInput) searchInput.addEventListener('input',  applyFilters);
            if (priceMin)    priceMin.addEventListener('input',     applyFilters);
            if (priceMax)    priceMax.addEventListener('input',     applyFilters);
            catChecks.forEach(function (cb)  { cb.addEventListener('change', applyFilters); });
            condChecks.forEach(function (cb) { cb.addEventListener('change', applyFilters); });

            function resetAll() {
                if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
                if (priceMin)    priceMin.value    = priceMin.min  || 0;
                if (priceMax)    priceMax.value    = priceMax.max  || 100000;
                catChecks.forEach(function (cb)  { cb.checked = false; });
                condChecks.forEach(function (cb) { cb.checked = false; });
                applyFilters();
            }

            var rb1 = document.getElementById('resetFilters');
            var rb2 = document.getElementById('resetFilters2');
            if (rb1) rb1.addEventListener('click', resetAll);
            if (rb2) rb2.addEventListener('click', resetAll);

            var toggleBtn = document.getElementById('fyFilterToggle');
            var sidebar   = document.getElementById('fySidebar');
            if (toggleBtn && sidebar) {
                toggleBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    sidebar.classList.toggle('fy-sidebar--open');
                    toggleBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded',
                        sidebar.classList.contains('fy-sidebar--open').toString());
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

@if (Model.ShowRequestId)
{
    <p>
        <strong>Request ID:</strong> <code>@Model.RequestId</code>
    </p>
}

<h3>Development Mode</h3>
<p>
    Swapping to <strong>Development</strong> environment will display more detailed information about the error that occurred.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>The Development environment shouldn't be enabled for deployed applications.</strong>
    It can result in displaying sensitive information from exceptions to end users.
    For local debugging, enable the <strong>Development</strong> environment by setting the <strong>ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT</strong> environment variable to <strong>Development</strong>
    and restarting the app.
</p>

--- Views/Shared/_Navbar.cshtml ---

@using System.Security.Claims
@using ThriftLoop.Repositories.Interface
@inject IShopRepository ShopRepo

@{
    var userEmail = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.Email)?.Value
                        ?? User.Identity?.Name
                        ?? string.Empty;
    var displayName = userEmail.Contains('@') ? userEmail.Split('@')[0] : userEmail;
    var currentPath = Context.Request.Path.Value ?? string.Empty;

    // Resolve live shop name for the navbar pill.
    // Done via @inject so it's always current — no stale cookie value.
    var shopLabel = "My Shop";
    if (User.IsInRole("Seller"))
    {
        var rawId = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier)?.Value;
        if (int.TryParse(rawId, out var navUserId))
        {
            var shop = await ShopRepo.GetByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(shop?.ShopName))
                shopLabel = shop.ShopName;
        }
    }
}

<nav class="tl-nav">
    <div class="tl-nav__inner">

        @* Logo *@
        <a asp-controller="Home" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__logo">ThriftLoop</a>

        <ul class="tl-nav__links" role="list">
            <li>
                <a asp-controller="Home"
                   asp-action="Index"
                   class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath == "/" || currentPath.StartsWith("/Home", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                    For You
                </a>
            </li>
            <li class="tl-nav__divider" aria-hidden="true"></li>
            <li>
                <a asp-controller="Sellers"
                   asp-action="Index"
                   class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Sellers", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                    Sellers
                </a>
            </li>
            <li class="tl-nav__divider" aria-hidden="true"></li>
            <li>
                <a asp-controller="Items"
                   asp-action="Index"
                   class="tl-nav__link @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Items", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__link--active" : "")">
                    My Listings
                </a>
            </li>
        </ul>

        @* ── Right side: My Shop pill + user dropdown ────────────────────────── *@
        <div class="tl-nav__user">
            @if (User.Identity?.IsAuthenticated == true)
            {
                @* My Shop pill — immediately left of the user dropdown, Sellers only *@
                @if (User.IsInRole("Seller"))
                {
                    <a asp-controller="Shop"
                       asp-action="Mine"
                       class="tl-nav__shop-btn @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Shop", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-nav__shop-btn--active" : "")">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8 1a2.5 2.5 0 00-2.5 2.5H3.5A1.5 1.5 0 002 5v8.5A1.5 1.5 0 003.5 15h9a1.5 1.5 0 001.5-1.5V5a1.5 1.5 0 00-1.5-1.5h-2A2.5 2.5 0 008 1zm0 1.5A1 1 0 019 3.5v0H7v0A1 1 0 018 2.5zm-2.5 2H4a.5.5 0 00-.5.5v8a.5.5 0 00.5.5h8a.5.5 0 00.5-.5V5a.5.5 0 00-.5-.5h-1.5v.75a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V4.5h-2v.75a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V4.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        @shopLabel
                    </a>
                }

                @* User dropdown *@
                <div class="tl-nav__dropdown">
                    <button class="tl-nav__dropdown-toggle" id="userDropdown" aria-expanded="false">
                        <span class="tl-nav__avatar" title="@userEmail">@char.ToUpper(displayName[0])</span>
                        <span class="tl-nav__name">@displayName</span>
                        <svg class="tl-nav__dropdown-chevron" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16">

                                </svg>
                                Sign out
                            </button>
                        </form>
                    </div>
                </div>
            }
            else
            {
                <div class="tl-nav__auth">
                    <a asp-controller="Auth" asp-action="Login" class="tl-nav__auth-link">Sign in</a>
                    <a asp-controller="Auth" asp-action="Register" class="tl-nav__auth-link tl-nav__auth-link--primary">Sign up</a>
                </div>
            }
        </div>

    </div>
</nav>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        const dropdownToggle = document.getElementById('userDropdown');
        const dropdownMenu   = document.getElementById('userDropdownMenu');

        if (dropdownToggle && dropdownMenu) {
            dropdownToggle.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                const isExpanded = this.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
                this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', !isExpanded);
                dropdownMenu.classList.toggle('show');
            });

            document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                if (!dropdownToggle.contains(e.target) && !dropdownMenu.contains(e.target)) {
                    dropdownToggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                    dropdownMenu.classList.remove('show');
                }
            });
        }
    });
</script>

                </svg>
                Images
                <span class="ic-card__label-hint">Up to @ItemConstants.MaxImagesPerListing photos · First is the cover</span>
            </div>

            <div class="ic-images" id="imageGrid"></div>

        @* ── SECTION 3: Variants ─────────────────────────────────────────────── *@

                    <div class="ic-card__label" style="margin-bottom:4px">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13" aria-hidden="true">
                            <path d="M11.28 3.22a.75.75 0 010 1.06L9.56 6l1.72 1.72a.75.75 0 11-1.06 1.06L8.5 7.06 6.78 8.78a.75.75 0 01-1.06-1.06L7.44 6 5.72 4.28a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06L8.5 4.94l1.72-1.72a.75.75 0 011.06 0zM2.5 6a.5.5 0 00-.5.5v3a.5.5 0 001 0v-3a.5.5 0 00-.5-.5zm11 0a.5.5 0 00-.5.5v3a.5.5 0 001 0v-3a.5.5 0 00-.5-.5z" />

                        Variants &amp; Inventory

                    <p class="ic-card__label-hint ic-card__label-hint--block">
                        Each variant is a colour, style, or option. Add sizes and stock quantities under each.
                    </p>
                </div>
                <button type="button" class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost" id="addVariantBtn" style="flex-shrink:0">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path d="M7.75 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75V7h4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H8.5v4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V8.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H7V2.75A.75.75 0 017.75 2z" />

    @* SKU row template ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
    <template id="skuTemplate">
        <div class="ic-sku-row">
            <select class="ic-field__select ic-sku__size">
                <option value="">No size</option>
                @foreach (var sz in ItemConstants.Sizes)
                {
                    <option value="@sz">@sz</option>
                }
            </select>
            <div class="ic-sku__price-wrap">
                <span class="ic-sku__currency">₱</span>
                <input type="number" class="ic-field__input ic-sku__price"
                       placeholder="0.00" min="0.01" step="0.01" />
            </div>
            <input type="number" class="ic-field__input ic-sku__qty"
                   placeholder="Qty" min="1" max="9999" step="1" />
            <button type="button" class="ic-sku__remove" aria-label="Remove row">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12">
                    <path d="M3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 011.06 0L8 6.94l3.22-3.22a.75.75 0 111.06 1.06L9.06 8l3.22 3.22a.75.75 0 11-1.06 1.06L8 9.06l-3.22 3.22a.75.75 0 01-1.06-1.06L6.94 8 3.72 4.78a.75.75 0 010-1.06z" />
                </svg>
            </button>
        </div>
    </template>

    <script>
            (function () {
                'use strict';

                const AF_TOKEN      = document.getElementById('afToken').value;
                const SHOP_ID       = parseInt(document.getElementById('shopId').value);
                const MAX_IMAGES    = @ItemConstants.MaxImagesPerListing;
                const MAX_VARIANTS  = 10;
                const CREATE_URL     = '/Shop/Create';
                const IMG_UPLOAD_URL = '/Shop/SaveListingImage';

                // ── State ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
                const imageFiles = new Array(MAX_IMAGES).fill(null);
                let variantCount = 0;

                // ── Helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
                function showError(elId, msg) {
                    const el = document.getElementById(elId);
                    if (!el) return;
                    el.textContent = msg;
                    el.hidden = !msg;
                }
                function showGlobal(msg) {
                    const banner = document.getElementById('globalError');
                    document.getElementById('globalErrorText').textContent = msg;
                    banner.hidden = !msg;
                    if (msg) banner.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
                }
                async function postJson(url, body) {
                    const res = await fetch(url, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                        body: JSON.stringify(body)
                    });
                    return res.json();
                }
                async function uploadFile(url, formData) {
                    const res = await fetch(url, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                        body: formData
                    });
                    return res.json();
                }

                // ── Image slots ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
                const imageGrid = document.getElementById('imageGrid');

                function renderImageSlots() {
                    imageGrid.innerHTML = '';
                    for (let i = 0; i < MAX_IMAGES; i++) {
                        const slot = document.createElement('label');
                        slot.className = 'ic-image-slot' + (i === 0 ? ' ic-image-slot--cover' : '');
                        slot.title = i === 0 ? 'Cover image' : `Image ${i + 1}`;

                        const input = document.createElement('input');
                        input.type = 'file';
                        input.accept = 'image/jpeg,image/png,image/webp,image/gif';
                        input.className = 'ic-image-slot__input';
                        input.dataset.slot = i;

                        if (imageFiles[i]) {
                            const img = document.createElement('img');
                            img.src = URL.createObjectURL(imageFiles[i]);
                            img.className = 'ic-image-slot__preview';
                            slot.appendChild(img);
                            if (i === 0) {
                                const badge = document.createElement('span');
                                badge.className = 'ic-image-slot__badge';
                                badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                                slot.appendChild(badge);
                            }
                        } else {
                            const icon = document.createElement('div');
                            icon.className = 'ic-image-slot__empty';
                            icon.innerHTML = `
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5"
                                     width="22" height="22" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"
                                          d="M12 16.5V9.75m0 0l3 3m-3-3l-3 3M6.75 19.5a4.5 4.5 0
                                             01-1.41-8.775 5.25 5.25 0 0110.233-2.33 3 3 0
                                             013.758 3.848A3.752 3.752 0 0118 19.5H6.75z"/>
                                </svg>
                                <span>${i === 0 ? 'Cover' : '+'}</span>`;
                            slot.appendChild(icon);
                        }

                        input.addEventListener('change', () => {
                            const file = input.files[0];
                            if (!file) return;
                            if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) { showError('errImages', `Image ${i + 1} exceeds 5 MB.`); return; }
                            showError('errImages', '');
                            imageFiles[i] = file;
                            renderImageSlots();
                        });

                        slot.appendChild(input);
                        imageGrid.appendChild(slot);
                    }
                }
                renderImageSlots();

                // ── Variant builder ────────────────────────────────────────────────
                const variantList   = document.getElementById('variantList');
                const addVariantBtn = document.getElementById('addVariantBtn');
                const skuTemplate   = document.getElementById('skuTemplate');

                function addVariant() {
                    if (variantCount >= MAX_VARIANTS) {
                        showError('errVariants', `Maximum ${MAX_VARIANTS} variants allowed.`);
                        return;
                    }
                    const vid  = ++variantCount;
                    const card = document.createElement('div');
                    card.className   = 'ic-variant-card';
                    card.dataset.vid = vid;

                    card.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="ic-variant-header">
                            <div class="ic-field" style="flex:1">
                                <label class="ic-field__label" for="vname-${vid}">Variant Name</label>
                                <input id="vname-${vid}" type="text" class="ic-field__input ic-variant__name"
                                       placeholder="e.g. Red, Navy, Classic Fit" maxlength="50" autocomplete="off" />
                                <p class="ic-field__error ic-variant__name-error" hidden></p>
                            </div>
                            <button type="button" class="ic-variant__remove" aria-label="Remove variant">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13">
                                    <path d="M11 1.75V3h2.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H5V1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h2.5C10.216 0 11 .784 11 1.75zM4.496 6.675a.75.75 0 10-1.492.15l.66 6.6A1.75 1.75 0 005.405 15h5.19a1.75 1.75 0 001.741-1.575l.66-6.6a.75.75 0 10-1.492-.15l-.66 6.6a.25.25 0 01-.249.225H5.405a.25.25 0 01-.249-.225l-.66-6.6z"/>
                                </svg>
                            </button>
                        </div>
                        <div class="ic-sku-list">
                            <div class="ic-sku-header">
                                <span>Size</span><span>Price</span><span>Qty</span><span></span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <button type="button" class="tl-btn tl-btn--ghost ic-add-sku" style="margin-top:10px;font-size:.75rem;padding:6px 12px">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="11" height="11">
                                <path d="M7.75 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75V7h4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H8.5v4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V8.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H7V2.75A.75.75 0 017.75 2z"/>
                            </svg>
                            Add Size / SKU
                        </button>
                        <p class="ic-field__error ic-variant__sku-error" hidden></p>`;

                    card.querySelector('.ic-variant__remove').addEventListener('click', () => {
                        card.remove();
                        showError('errVariants', '');
                    });
                    card.querySelector('.ic-add-sku').addEventListener('click', () => {
                        addSku(card.querySelector('.ic-sku-list'));
                    });

                    variantList.appendChild(card);
                    showError('errVariants', '');
                    addSku(card.querySelector('.ic-sku-list'));
                    card.querySelector('.ic-variant__name').focus();
                }

                function addSku(skuList) {
                    const row = skuTemplate.content.cloneNode(true).querySelector('.ic-sku-row');
                    row.querySelector('.ic-sku__remove').addEventListener('click', () => row.remove());
                    skuList.appendChild(row);
                }

                addVariantBtn.addEventListener('click', addVariant);
                addVariant();

                // ── Validation ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
                function validateAndBuild() {
                    let valid = true;
                    const title     = document.getElementById('itemTitle').value.trim();
                    const desc      = document.getElementById('itemDesc').value.trim();
                    const category  = document.getElementById('itemCategory').value;
                    const condition = document.getElementById('itemCondition').value;

                    ['errTitle','errDesc','errCategory','errCondition','errVariants','errImages'].forEach(id => showError(id, ''));
                    showGlobal('');

                    if (!title)     { showError('errTitle',     'Title is required.');             valid = false; }
                    if (!desc)      { showError('errDesc',      'Description is required.');       valid = false; }
                    if (!category)  { showError('errCategory',  'Please select a category.');      valid = false; }
                    if (!condition) { showError('errCondition', 'Please select a condition.');     valid = false; }
                    if (imageFiles.filter(Boolean).length === 0) { showError('errImages', 'Add at least one image.'); valid = false; }

                    const variantCards = variantList.querySelectorAll('.ic-variant-card');
                    if (variantCards.length === 0) { showError('errVariants', 'Add at least one variant.'); valid = false; }

                    const variants = [];
                    variantCards.forEach(card => {
                        const name    = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__name').value.trim();
                        const nameErr = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__name-error');
                        const skuErr  = card.querySelector('.ic-variant__sku-error');
                        nameErr.hidden = skuErr.hidden = true;

                        if (!name) { nameErr.textContent = 'Variant name is required.'; nameErr.hidden = false; valid = false; }

                        const skus = [];
                        card.querySelectorAll('.ic-sku-row').forEach(row => {
                            const size  = row.querySelector('.ic-sku__size').value;
                            const price = parseFloat(row.querySelector('.ic-sku__price').value);
                            const qty   = parseInt(row.querySelector('.ic-sku__qty').value, 10);
                            if (isNaN(price) || price <= 0) { skuErr.textContent = 'All SKUs need a valid price.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; return; }
                            if (isNaN(qty)   || qty < 1)   { skuErr.textContent = 'All SKUs need a valid quantity.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; return; }
                            skus.push({ size: size || null, price, quantity: qty });
                        });
                        if (skus.length === 0) { skuErr.textContent = 'Add at least one SKU.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; }
                        variants.push({ name, skus });
                    });

                    if (!valid) return null;
                    return { shopId: SHOP_ID, title, description: desc, category, condition, variants };
                }

                // ── Publish ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
                document.getElementById('publishBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
                    const payload = validateAndBuild();
                    if (!payload) return;

                    const btn = document.getElementById('publishBtn');
                    btn.disabled    = true;
                    btn.textContent = 'Publishing…';

                    const createRes = await postJson(CREATE_URL, payload);
                    if (!createRes.ok) {
                        showGlobal(createRes.error ?? 'Failed to create item.');
                        btn.disabled    = false;
                        btn.innerHTML   = `<svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="13" height="13"><path d="M8.75 1.75a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0V8H3.75a.75.75 0 000 1.5h3.5V13a.75.75 0 001.5 0V9.5h3.5a.75.75 0 000-1.5H8.75V1.75z"/></svg> Publish Item`;
                        return;
                    }

                    const itemId = createRes.itemId;
                    const selectedFiles = imageFiles.map((f, i) => ({ file: f, slot: i })).filter(x => x.file !== null);

                    for (const { file, slot } of selectedFiles) {
                        btn.textContent = `Uploading image ${slot + 1}…`;
                        const fd = new FormData();
                        fd.append('itemId', itemId);
                        fd.append('slot',   slot);
                        fd.append('file',   file);
                        const imgRes = await uploadFile(IMG_UPLOAD_URL, fd);
                        if (!imgRes.ok) {
                            showGlobal(`Item created but image ${slot + 1} failed: ${imgRes.error}`);
                            btn.disabled    = false;
                            btn.textContent = 'Publish Item';
                            return;
                        }
                    }

                    window.location.href = `/Shop/Mine`;
                });

            }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                else
                {
                    <div class="detail-actions" id="buyerActions">
                        <button type="button"
                                class="tl-btn tl-btn--primary detail-actions__btn"
                                id="buyNowBtn"
                                disabled
                                style="width:100%; padding:13px 20px; font-size:.9rem">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                <path d="M0 1.75A.75.75 0 01.75 1h1.628a1.75 1.75 0 011.734 1.51L4.358 4h9.109a.75.75 0 01.72.96l-1.5 5.25a.75.75 0 01-.72.54H5.744l.239 1.185A.25.25 0 006.22 12h7.28a.75.75 0 010 1.5H6.22a1.75 1.75 0 01-1.717-1.424L2.637 2.773A.25.25 0 002.395 2.5H.75A.75.75 0 010 1.75zM6 14.5a1 1 0 112 0 1 1 0 01-2 0zm6.5-1a1 1 0 100 2 1 1 0 000-2z" />
                            </svg>
                            Buy Now
                        </button>

                @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)

    <script>
            (function () {
                'use strict';

                // ── Variant / SKU data ──────────────────────────────────────────────
                const rawData = document.getElementById('variantData');
                if (!rawData) return;

                const variants       = JSON.parse(rawData.textContent);
                const variantChipsEl = document.getElementById('variantChips');
                const skuSection     = document.getElementById('skuSection');
                const skuChipsEl     = document.getElementById('skuChips');
                const priceEl        = document.getElementById('selectedPrice');
                const priceLabelEl   = document.getElementById('priceLabel');
                const variantReqEl   = document.getElementById('variantRequired');
                const skuReqEl       = document.getElementById('skuRequired');
                const qtySection     = document.getElementById('qtySection');
                const qtyInput       = document.getElementById('qtyInput');
                const qtyDecBtn      = document.getElementById('qtyDec');
                const qtyIncBtn      = document.getElementById('qtyInc');
                const qtyStock       = document.getElementById('qtyStock');
                const buyNowBtn      = document.getElementById('buyNowBtn');

                let selectedVariantId = null;
                let selectedSkuId     = null;

                // ── Variant chip click ──────────────────────────────────────────────
                variantChipsEl?.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    const chip = e.target.closest('.vp-chip');
                    if (!chip) return;

                    variantChipsEl.querySelectorAll('.vp-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('vp-chip--active'));
                    chip.classList.add('vp-chip--active');

                    selectedVariantId = parseInt(chip.dataset.variantId);
                    selectedSkuId     = null;
                    if (variantReqEl) variantReqEl.hidden = true;
                    hideQtyPicker();
                    if (buyNowBtn) buyNowBtn.disabled = true;

                    const variant = variants.find(v => v.variantId === selectedVariantId);
                    if (!variant) return;

                    skuChipsEl.innerHTML = '';
                    variant.skus.forEach(sku => {
                        const btn = document.createElement('button');
                        btn.type             = 'button';
                        btn.className        = 'vp-chip' + (sku.isAvailable ? '' : ' vp-chip--disabled');
                        btn.dataset.skuId    = sku.skuId;
                        btn.dataset.price    = sku.price;
                        btn.dataset.quantity = sku.quantity;
                        btn.disabled         = !sku.isAvailable;
                        btn.textContent      = sku.size || 'One size';
                        if (!sku.isAvailable) btn.title = 'Out of stock';
                        skuChipsEl.appendChild(btn);
                    });

                    skuSection.removeAttribute('hidden');

                    const lowestAvailable = variant.skus
                        .filter(s => s.isAvailable)
                        .reduce((min, s) => s.price < min ? s.price : min, Infinity);

                    if (lowestAvailable < Infinity) {
                        priceEl.textContent      = '₱' + lowestAvailable.toLocaleString('en-PH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                        priceLabelEl.textContent = 'Starting price';
                    }
                });

                // ── SKU chip click ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
                skuChipsEl?.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    const chip = e.target.closest('.vp-chip:not(.vp-chip--disabled)');
                    if (!chip) return;

                    skuChipsEl.querySelectorAll('.vp-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('vp-chip--active'));
                    chip.classList.add('vp-chip--active');

                    selectedSkuId = parseInt(chip.dataset.skuId);
                    if (skuReqEl) skuReqEl.hidden = true;

                    const unitPrice = parseFloat(chip.dataset.price);
                    const maxQty    = parseInt(chip.dataset.quantity) || 1;

                    priceEl.textContent      = '₱' + unitPrice.toLocaleString('en-PH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    priceLabelEl.textContent = maxQty + ' available';

                    showQtyPicker(maxQty, unitPrice);
                    if (buyNowBtn) buyNowBtn.disabled = false;
                });

                // ── Quantity picker ────────────────────────────────────────────────
                function showQtyPicker(maxQty, unitPrice) {
                    if (!qtySection) return;
                    qtyInput.max   = maxQty;
                    qtyInput.value = 1;
                    qtyStock.textContent = maxQty + ' in stock';
                    qtySection.removeAttribute('hidden');
                    updateQtyButtons();
                    updatePriceForQty(unitPrice, 1);
                }
                function hideQtyPicker() {
                    if (qtySection) qtySection.setAttribute('hidden', '');
                }
                function updateQtyButtons() {
                    if (!qtyInput) return;
                    const v   = parseInt(qtyInput.value) || 1;
                    const max = parseInt(qtyInput.max)   || 1;
                    if (qtyDecBtn) qtyDecBtn.disabled = v <= 1;
                    if (qtyIncBtn) qtyIncBtn.disabled = v >= max;
                }
                function updatePriceForQty(unitPrice, qty) {
                    if (!priceEl) return;
                    if (qty > 1) {
                        priceEl.textContent      = '₱' + (unitPrice * qty).toLocaleString('en-PH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                        priceLabelEl.textContent = qty + ' × ₱' + unitPrice.toLocaleString('en-PH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    } else {
                        priceEl.textContent      = '₱' + unitPrice.toLocaleString('en-PH', { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                        priceLabelEl.textContent = (parseInt(qtyInput?.max || 1)) + ' available';
                    }
                }
                function currentUnitPrice() {
                    const activeChip = skuChipsEl?.querySelector('.vp-chip--active');
                    return activeChip ? parseFloat(activeChip.dataset.price) : 0;
                }

                qtyDecBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    const v = parseInt(qtyInput.value) || 1;
                    if (v > 1) { qtyInput.value = v - 1; updateQtyButtons(); updatePriceForQty(currentUnitPrice(), v - 1); }
                });
                qtyIncBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    const v = parseInt(qtyInput.value) || 1, max = parseInt(qtyInput.max) || 1;
                    if (v < max) { qtyInput.value = v + 1; updateQtyButtons(); updatePriceForQty(currentUnitPrice(), v + 1); }
                });
                qtyInput?.addEventListener('input', () => {
                    let v = Math.max(1, Math.min(parseInt(qtyInput.value) || 1, parseInt(qtyInput.max) || 1));
                    qtyInput.value = v;
                    updateQtyButtons();
                    updatePriceForQty(currentUnitPrice(), v);
                });

                // ── Buy Now ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
                buyNowBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    let valid = true;
                    if (!selectedVariantId) { if (variantReqEl) variantReqEl.hidden = false; valid = false; }
                    if (!selectedSkuId)     { if (skuReqEl)     skuReqEl.hidden     = false; valid = false; }
                    if (!valid) return;
                    const qty = parseInt(qtyInput?.value) || 1;
                    window.location.href = '/Orders/ShopCheckout?skuId=' + selectedSkuId + '&quantity=' + qty;
                });

                // ── Image gallery ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
                const mainImg = document.getElementById('mainGalleryImg');
                const thumbs  = document.querySelectorAll('.gallery-thumb');
                const counter = document.getElementById('galleryCounter');
                const prevBtn = document.getElementById('galleryPrev');
                const nextBtn = document.getElementById('galleryNext');

                const urls = Array.from(thumbs).map(t => t.dataset.src);
                let current = 0;

                function goTo(idx) {
                    if (!mainImg || urls.length === 0) return;
                    const next = (idx + urls.length) % urls.length;
                    if (next === current) return;

                    // Crossfade
                    mainImg.classList.add('fading');
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        current     = next;
                        mainImg.src = urls[current];
                        mainImg.classList.remove('fading');
                        thumbs.forEach((t, i) => t.classList.toggle('gallery-thumb--active', i === current));
                        if (counter) counter.textContent = (current + 1) + ' / ' + urls.length;
                    }, 130);
                }

                thumbs.forEach((t, i) => t.addEventListener('click', () => goTo(i)));
                prevBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => goTo(current - 1));
                nextBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => goTo(current + 1));

                // Keyboard navigation
                document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
                    if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft')  goTo(current - 1);
                    if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') goTo(current + 1);
                });

                // Swipe support
                let touchStartX = 0;
                const galleryEl = document.getElementById('galleryMain');
                galleryEl?.addEventListener('touchstart', e => { touchStartX = e.touches[0].clientX; }, { passive: true });
                galleryEl?.addEventListener('touchend',   e => {
                    const dx = e.changedTouches[0].clientX - touchStartX;
                    if (Math.abs(dx) > 40) goTo(dx < 0 ? current + 1 : current - 1);
                });

            }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    ViewData["Title"] = "Edit — " + Model.Title;
    Layout = null;

    var variantJson = System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(
        Model.Variants.Select(v => new
        {
            variantId = v.VariantId,
            name = v.Name,
            skus = v.Skus.Select(s => new
            {
                skuId = s.SkuId,
                size = s.Size,
                price = s.Price,
                quantity = s.Quantity
            })
        })
    );
}

    @* SKU row template *@
    <template id="skuTemplate">
        <div class="edit-sku-row">
            <select class="edit-field__select edit-sku__size">
                <option value="">No size</option>
                @foreach (var sz in ShopItemEditViewModel.Sizes)
                {
                    <option value="@sz">@sz</option>
                }
            </select>
            <div class="edit-price-input">
                <span class="edit-price-input__symbol">₱</span>
                <input type="number" class="edit-field__input edit-sku__price"
                       placeholder="0.00" min="0.01" step="0.01" />
            </div>
            <input type="number" class="edit-field__input edit-sku__qty"
                   placeholder="Qty" min="1" max="9999" step="1" />
            <button type="button" class="edit-sku__remove" aria-label="Remove SKU">
                <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor">
                    <path d="M3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 011.06 0L8 6.94l3.22-3.22a.75.75 0 111.06 1.06L9.06 8l3.22 3.22a.75.75 0 11-1.06 1.06L8 9.06l-3.22 3.22a.75.75 0 01-1.06-1.06L6.94 8 3.72 4.78a.75.75 0 010-1.06z"/>
                </svg>
            </button>
        </div>
    </template>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            const AF_TOKEN         = document.getElementById('afToken').value;
            const ITEM_ID          = parseInt(document.getElementById('itemId').value);
            const MAX_IMAGES       = @ItemConstants.MaxImagesPerListing;
            const EDIT_URL         = '/Shop/Edit';
            const IMG_UPLOAD_URL   = '/Shop/SaveListingImage';
            const IMG_REMOVE_URL   = '/Shop/RemoveListingImage';

            const EXISTING_VARIANTS = @Html.Raw(variantJson);
            const EXISTING_IMAGES   = @Html.Raw(System.Text.Json.JsonSerializer.Serialize(Model.ImageUrls));

            const imageSlots = [];

            for (let i = 0; i < MAX_IMAGES; i++) {
                if (i < EXISTING_IMAGES.length && EXISTING_IMAGES[i]) {
                    imageSlots.push({ type: 'existing', url: EXISTING_IMAGES[i] });
                } else {
                    imageSlots.push({ type: 'empty' });
                }
            }

            function showError(id, msg) {
                const el = document.getElementById(id);
                if (!el) return;
                el.textContent = msg;
                el.hidden = !msg;
            }

            function showGlobal(msg) {
                const banner = document.getElementById('globalError');
                document.getElementById('globalErrorText').textContent = msg;
                banner.hidden = !msg;
                if (msg) banner.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
            }

            async function postJson(url, body) {
                const res = await fetch(url, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                    body: JSON.stringify(body)
                });
                return res.json();
            }

            async function postForm(url, fd) {
                const res = await fetch(url, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                    body: fd
                });
                return res.json();
            }

            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            //  IMAGE GRID
            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            const imageGrid = document.getElementById('imageGrid');

            function renderImageGrid() {
                imageGrid.innerHTML = '';
                imageSlots.forEach((slot, i) => {
                    const label = document.createElement('label');
                    label.className = 'edit-image-slot' + (i === 0 ? ' edit-image-slot--cover' : '');

                    if (slot.type === 'empty') {
                        const input = document.createElement('input');
                        input.type = 'file';
                        input.accept = 'image/jpeg,image/png,image/webp,image/gif';
                        input.className = 'edit-image-slot__input';
                        input.addEventListener('change', () => handleNewImage(i, input.files[0]));
                        label.appendChild(input);

                        const empty = document.createElement('div');
                        empty.className = 'edit-image-slot__empty';
                        empty.innerHTML = `<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="24" height="24">
                            <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M12 16.5V9.75m0 0l3 3m-3-3l-3 3M6.75 19.5a4.5 4.5 0 01-1.41-8.775 5.25 5.25 0 0110.233-2.33 3 3 0 013.758 3.848A3.752 3.752 0 0118 19.5H6.75z"/>
                        </svg><span>${i === 0 ? 'Cover' : 'Add'}</span>`;
                        label.appendChild(empty);
                    } else {
                        const img = document.createElement('img');
                        img.src = slot.type === 'existing' ? slot.url : URL.createObjectURL(slot.file);
                        img.className = 'edit-image-slot__preview';
                        label.appendChild(img);

                        if (i === 0) {
                            const badge = document.createElement('span');
                            badge.className = 'edit-image-slot__badge';
                            badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                            label.appendChild(badge);
                        }

                        const removeBtn = document.createElement('button');
                        removeBtn.type = 'button';
                        removeBtn.className = 'edit-image-slot__remove';
                        removeBtn.innerHTML = '×';
                        removeBtn.addEventListener('click', e => { e.preventDefault(); removeSlot(i); });
                        label.appendChild(removeBtn);
                    }

                    imageGrid.appendChild(label);
                });
            }

            async function handleNewImage(slot, file) {
                if (!file) return;
                if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) { showError('errImages', 'Image exceeds 5 MB.'); return; }
                showError('errImages', '');

                const fd = new FormData();
                fd.append('itemId', ITEM_ID);
                fd.append('slot', slot);
                fd.append('file', file);
                const res = await postForm(IMG_UPLOAD_URL, fd);

                if (!res.ok) { showError('errImages', res.error); return; }

                imageSlots[slot] = { type: 'existing', url: res.url };
                renderImageGrid();
            }

            async function removeSlot(slot) {
                const s = imageSlots[slot];
                if (s.type === 'existing') {
                    const fd = new FormData();
                    fd.append('itemId', ITEM_ID);
                    fd.append('url', s.url);
                    await postForm(IMG_REMOVE_URL, fd);
                }
                imageSlots[slot] = { type: 'empty' };
                renderImageGrid();
            }

            renderImageGrid();

            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            //  VARIANT BUILDER
            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            const variantList   = document.getElementById('variantList');
            const addVariantBtn = document.getElementById('addVariantBtn');
            const skuTemplate   = document.getElementById('skuTemplate');

            function addVariant(existingVariant) {
                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = 'edit-variant-card';

                const vId = existingVariant?.variantId ?? null;
                if (vId) card.dataset.variantId = vId;

                card.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="edit-variant-header">
                        <div class="edit-variant-name">
                            <label class="edit-field__label">Variant Name</label>
                            <input type="text" class="edit-field__input edit-variant__name"
                                   value="${escapeHtml(existingVariant?.name ?? '')}"
                                   placeholder="e.g., Red, Navy, Classic Fit" maxlength="50" />
                            <p class="edit-field__error edit-variant__name-error" hidden></p>
                        </div>
                        <button type="button" class="edit-variant__remove" aria-label="Remove variant">
                            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor">
                                <path d="M11 1.75V3h2.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H5V1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h2.5C10.216 0 11 .784 11 1.75zM4.496 6.675a.75.75 0 10-1.492.15l.66 6.6A1.75 1.75 0 005.405 15h5.19a1.75 1.75 0 001.741-1.575l.66-6.6a.75.75 0 10-1.492-.15l-.66 6.6a.25.25 0 01-.249.225H5.405a.25.25 0 01-.249-.225l-.66-6.6z"/>
                            </svg>
                        </button>
                    </div>
                    <div class="edit-sku-table">
                        <div class="edit-sku-table__header">
                            <span>Size</span>
                            <span>Price</span>
                            <span>Quantity</span>
                            <span></span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="edit-sku-table__body"></div>
                    </div>
                    <button type="button" class="edit-btn edit-btn--small edit-btn--outline edit-add-sku">
                        <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor">
                            <path d="M8 2a.75.75 0 01.75.75V7h4.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H8.75v4.25a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0V8.5H3a.75.75 0 010-1.5h4.25V2.75A.75.75 0 018 2z"/>
                        </svg>
                        Add SKU
                    </button>
                    <p class="edit-field__error edit-variant__sku-error" hidden></p>`;

                const skuBody = card.querySelector('.edit-sku-table__body');
                card.querySelector('.edit-variant__remove').addEventListener('click', () => card.remove());
                card.querySelector('.edit-add-sku').addEventListener('click', () => addSku(skuBody, null));

                variantList.appendChild(card);

                if (existingVariant?.skus?.length) {
                    existingVariant.skus.forEach(s => addSku(skuBody, s));
                } else {
                    addSku(skuBody, null);
                }
            }

            function escapeHtml(str) {
                if (!str) return '';
                return str.replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
                    if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
                    if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
                    if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
                    return m;
                });
            }

            function addSku(skuBody, existingSku) {
                const row = skuTemplate.content.cloneNode(true).querySelector('.edit-sku-row');
                if (existingSku?.skuId) row.dataset.skuId = existingSku.skuId;

                const sizeSelect = row.querySelector('.edit-sku__size');
                const priceInput = row.querySelector('.edit-sku__price');
                const qtyInput   = row.querySelector('.edit-sku__qty');

                if (existingSku) {
                    if (existingSku.size) sizeSelect.value = existingSku.size;
                    priceInput.value = existingSku.price;
                    qtyInput.value   = existingSku.quantity;
                }

                row.querySelector('.edit-sku__remove').addEventListener('click', () => row.remove());
                skuBody.appendChild(row);
            }

            EXISTING_VARIANTS.forEach(v => addVariant(v));
            addVariantBtn.addEventListener('click', () => addVariant(null));

            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            //  SAVE
            // ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            function buildPayload() {
                let valid = true;

                const title     = document.getElementById('itemTitle').value.trim();
                const desc      = document.getElementById('itemDesc').value.trim();
                const category  = document.getElementById('itemCategory').value;
                const condition = document.getElementById('itemCondition').value;

                showError('errTitle', '');
                showError('errDesc', '');
                showError('errCategory', '');
                showError('errCondition', '');
                showError('errVariants', '');
                showGlobal('');

                if (!title)     { showError('errTitle',    'Title is required.');          valid = false; }
                if (!desc)      { showError('errDesc',     'Description is required.');    valid = false; }
                if (!category)  { showError('errCategory', 'Please select a category.');   valid = false; }
                if (!condition) { showError('errCondition','Please select a condition.');   valid = false; }

                const variantCards = variantList.querySelectorAll('.edit-variant-card');
                if (!variantCards.length) { showError('errVariants', 'Add at least one variant.'); valid = false; }

                const variants = [];
                variantCards.forEach(card => {
                    const nameInput = card.querySelector('.edit-variant__name');
                    const nameErr   = card.querySelector('.edit-variant__name-error');
                    const skuErr    = card.querySelector('.edit-variant__sku-error');
                    nameErr.hidden = skuErr.hidden = true;

                    const name = nameInput.value.trim();
                    if (!name) { nameErr.textContent = 'Variant name is required.'; nameErr.hidden = false; valid = false; }

                    const skus = [];
                    card.querySelectorAll('.edit-sku-row').forEach(row => {
                        const price = parseFloat(row.querySelector('.edit-sku__price').value);
                        const qty   = parseInt(row.querySelector('.edit-sku__qty').value, 10);
                        const size  = row.querySelector('.edit-sku__size').value;

                        if (isNaN(price) || price <= 0) { skuErr.textContent = 'All SKUs need a valid price.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; return; }
                        if (isNaN(qty)   || qty < 1)    { skuErr.textContent = 'All SKUs need a valid quantity.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; return; }

                        const skuId = row.dataset.skuId ? parseInt(row.dataset.skuId) : null;
                        skus.push({ skuId, size: size || null, price, quantity: qty });
                    });

                    if (!skus.length) { skuErr.textContent = 'Add at least one SKU.'; skuErr.hidden = false; valid = false; }

                    const variantId = card.dataset.variantId ? parseInt(card.dataset.variantId) : null;
                    variants.push({ variantId, name, skus });
                });

                if (!valid) return null;

                return { shopItemId: ITEM_ID, title, description: desc, category, condition, variants };
            }

            document.getElementById('saveBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
                const payload = buildPayload();
                if (!payload) return;

                const btn = document.getElementById('saveBtn');
                btn.disabled    = true;
                btn.innerHTML   = '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><path d="M12 6v6l4 2"/></svg>Saving...';
                
                const res = await postJson(EDIT_URL, payload);

                btn.disabled    = false;
                btn.innerHTML   = '<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor"><path d="M13.25 1.75a.75.75 0 011.5 0v3.5a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-3.5zM11.5 4.5a.75.75 0 010 1.5h-7a.75.75 0 010-1.5h7zM9.25 7.75a.75.75 0 011.5 0v3.5a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-3.5zM7.5 10.5a.75.75 0 010 1.5h-3a.75.75 0 010-1.5h3z"/></svg>Save Changes';

                if (!res.ok) { showGlobal(res.error ?? 'Failed to save changes.'); return; }

                window.location.href = `/Shop/Details/@Model.ItemId`;
            });
        }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                                    <path d="M11 1.75V3h2.25a.75.75 0 010 1.5H2.75a.75.75 0 010-1.5H5V1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h2.5C10.216 0 11 .784 11 1.75z" />
                                </svg>
                                Delete
