                    }
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    }

</div>

@if (isOwner)
{
    <input type="hidden" id="afToken" value="@afToken" />
    
    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            const SHOP_ID   = @Model.ShopId;
            const AF_TOKEN  = document.getElementById('afToken').value;
            const FIELD_URL = '/Shop/SaveField';
            const IMAGE_URL = '/Shop/SaveImage';

            // ── AJAX helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            async function saveTextField(field, value) {
                const res = await fetch(FIELD_URL, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ shopId: SHOP_ID, field, value })
                });
                return res.json();
            }

            async function uploadImage(field, file) {
                const fd = new FormData();
                fd.append('shopId', SHOP_ID);
                fd.append('field',  field);
                fd.append('file',   file);
                const res = await fetch(IMAGE_URL, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                    body: fd
                });
                return res.json();
            }

            // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            //  IMAGE MODAL
            // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            const backdrop    = document.getElementById('imgModalBackdrop');
            const modalTitle  = document.getElementById('imgModalTitle');
            const previewArea = document.getElementById('imgPreviewArea');
            const dropZone    = document.getElementById('imgDropZone');
            const fileInput   = document.getElementById('imgFileInput');
            const dropInner   = document.getElementById('imgDropInner');
            const saveBtn     = document.getElementById('imgModalSave');
            const cancelBtn   = document.getElementById('imgModalCancel');
            const closeBtn    = document.getElementById('imgModalClose');
            const errorEl     = document.getElementById('imgModalError');

            let activeField = null;
            let pendingFile = null;

            function openModal(field, currentUrl, title) {
                activeField      = field;
                pendingFile      = null;
                saveBtn.disabled = true;
                errorEl.hidden   = true;
                fileInput.value  = '';
                modalTitle.textContent = title;

                previewArea.innerHTML = '';
                if (currentUrl && currentUrl !== 'null') {
                    if (field === 'BannerUrl') {
                        const div = document.createElement('div');
                        div.className = 'sp-modal__banner-preview';
                        // Clean URL for preview (remove cache buster)
                        const cleanUrl = currentUrl.split('?')[0];
                        div.style.backgroundImage = `url('${cleanUrl}')`;
                        previewArea.appendChild(div);
                    } else {
                        const img = document.createElement('img');
                        const cleanUrl = currentUrl.split('?')[0];
                        img.src = cleanUrl;
                        img.className = 'sp-modal__logo-preview';
                        previewArea.appendChild(img);
                    }
                } else {
                    const empty = document.createElement('div');
                    empty.className = 'sp-modal__preview-empty';
                    empty.textContent = 'No image set — upload one below';
                    previewArea.appendChild(empty);
                }

                dropInner.querySelector('.sp-modal__drop-label').textContent = 'Click or drag an image here';
                backdrop.removeAttribute('hidden');
                dropZone.focus();
            }

            function closeModal() {
                backdrop.setAttribute('hidden', '');
                activeField = pendingFile = null;
            }

            closeBtn?.addEventListener('click',  closeModal);
            cancelBtn?.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
            backdrop?.addEventListener('click',  e => { if (e.target === backdrop) closeModal(); });
            document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') closeModal(); });

            // ── File selection ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function handleFile(file) {
                if (!file) return;
                const allowed = ['image/jpeg','image/png','image/webp','image/gif'];
                if (!allowed.includes(file.type)) { showModalError('Only JPEG, PNG, WebP, or GIF images are allowed.'); return; }
                if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024)  { showModalError('File exceeds the 5 MB limit.'); return; }

                errorEl.hidden     = true;
                pendingFile        = file;
                saveBtn.disabled   = false;

                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = e => {
                    previewArea.innerHTML = '';
                    if (activeField === 'BannerUrl') {
                        const div = document.createElement('div');
                        div.className = 'sp-modal__banner-preview';
                        div.style.backgroundImage = `url('${e.target.result}')`;
                        previewArea.appendChild(div);
                    } else {
                        const img = document.createElement('img');
                        img.src = e.target.result;
                        img.className = 'sp-modal__logo-preview';
                        previewArea.appendChild(img);
                    }
                };
                reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                dropInner.querySelector('.sp-modal__drop-label').textContent = file.name;
            }

            fileInput?.addEventListener('change', () => handleFile(fileInput.files[0]));
            dropZone?.addEventListener('dragover',  e => { e.preventDefault(); dropZone.classList.add('sp-modal__drop-zone--over'); });
            dropZone?.addEventListener('dragleave', ()  => dropZone.classList.remove('sp-modal__drop-zone--over'));
            dropZone?.addEventListener('drop', e => {
                e.preventDefault();
                dropZone.classList.remove('sp-modal__drop-zone--over');
                handleFile(e.dataTransfer.files[0]);
            });

            // ── Upload ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            saveBtn?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                if (!pendingFile || !activeField) return;
                
                const originalText = saveBtn.textContent;
                saveBtn.disabled    = true;
                saveBtn.textContent = 'Uploading…';
                errorEl.hidden      = true;

                try {
                    const res = await uploadImage(activeField, pendingFile);
                    
                    if (!res.ok) {
                        showModalError(res.error || 'Upload failed');
                        saveBtn.disabled = false;
                        saveBtn.textContent = originalText;
                        return;
                    }

                    // Add timestamp to prevent caching issues
                    const cacheBuster = `${res.url}?v=${Date.now()}`;

                    if (activeField === 'BannerUrl') {
                        const banner = document.getElementById('shopBanner');
                        banner.style.backgroundImage = `url('${cacheBuster}')`;
                        const placeholder = banner.querySelector('.sp-banner__placeholder');
                        if (placeholder) placeholder.remove();
                        // Store the clean URL for future reference
                        banner.setAttribute('data-original-bg', res.url);
                    } else {
                        // Handle logo update
                        const existingLogo = document.getElementById('shopLogoImg');
                        
                        if (existingLogo) {
                            if (existingLogo.tagName === 'DIV') {
                                // Replace placeholder div with img
                                const img = document.createElement('img');
                                img.src = cacheBuster;
                                img.id = 'shopLogoImg';
                                img.alt = 'Shop logo';
                                img.className = 'sp-identity__logo';
                                img.setAttribute('data-original-src', res.url);
                                existingLogo.replaceWith(img);
                            } else if (existingLogo.tagName === 'IMG') {
                                // Update existing img src
                                existingLogo.src = cacheBuster;
                                existingLogo.setAttribute('data-original-src', res.url);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Show success indicator
                    const tempMsg = document.createElement('div');
                    tempMsg.textContent = 'Image uploaded successfully!';
                    tempMsg.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;bottom:20px;right:20px;background:#0e6245;color:#fff;padding:10px 20px;border-radius:8px;z-index:1000;animation:fadeOut 2s ease forwards;';
                    document.body.appendChild(tempMsg);
                    setTimeout(() => tempMsg.remove(), 2000);
                    
                } catch (err) {
                    showModalError('Network error. Please try again.');
                    console.error('Upload error:', err);
                } finally {
                    saveBtn.disabled = false;
                    saveBtn.textContent = originalText;
                }
                
                closeModal();
            });

            function showModalError(msg) {
                errorEl.textContent = msg;
                errorEl.hidden      = false;
            }

            // ── Trigger: Banner & Logo clicks ───────────────────────────────────
            const bannerElement = document.getElementById('shopBanner');
            if (bannerElement) {
                bannerElement.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    const style = bannerElement.style.backgroundImage;
                    let current = null;
                    if (style && style !== 'none') {
                        current = style.replace(/^url\(['"]?/, '').replace(/['"]?\)$/, '').split('?')[0];
                    }
                    openModal('BannerUrl', current, 'Banner Image');
                });
            }

            const logoWrap = document.getElementById('shopLogoWrap');
            if (logoWrap) {
                const openLogo = () => {
                    const img = document.getElementById('shopLogoImg');
                    let current = null;
                    if (img && img.tagName === 'IMG') {
                        current = img.getAttribute('data-original-src') || img.src.split('?')[0];
                    }
                    openModal('LogoUrl', current, 'Logo Image');
                };
                logoWrap.addEventListener('click', openLogo);
                logoWrap.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
                    if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        openLogo();
                    }
                });
            }

            // Add fade-out animation for success message
            const style = document.createElement('style');
            style.textContent = `
                @@keyframes fadeOut {
                    0% { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
                    70% { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
                    100% { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(-20px); visibility: hidden; }
                }
            `;
            document.head.appendChild(style);

            // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            //  FORCE REFRESH IMAGES ON PAGE LOAD (CACHE BUSTING)
            // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            function refreshImagesWithCacheBuster() {
                // Refresh logo if it's an image
                const logo = document.getElementById('shopLogoImg');
                if (logo && logo.tagName === 'IMG' && logo.src) {
                    const originalSrc = logo.getAttribute('data-original-src') || logo.src.split('?')[0];
                    if (originalSrc && originalSrc !== '') {
                        logo.src = originalSrc + '?v=' + Date.now();
                    }
                }
                
                // Refresh banner if it has background image
                const banner = document.getElementById('shopBanner');
                if (banner && banner.style.backgroundImage) {
                    const bg = banner.style.backgroundImage;
                    const urlMatch = bg.match(/url\(['"]?([^'"]+)['"]?\)/);
                    if (urlMatch && urlMatch[1]) {
                        const cleanUrl = urlMatch[1].split('?')[0];
                        if (cleanUrl && cleanUrl !== '' && cleanUrl !== 'none') {
                            banner.style.backgroundImage = `url('${cleanUrl}?v=${Date.now()}')`;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            // Run on page load
            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', refreshImagesWithCacheBuster);
            } else {
                refreshImagesWithCacheBuster();
            }

            // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            //  INLINE TEXT EDITING (ShopName + Bio)
            // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
            document.querySelectorAll('.sp-inline--editable').forEach(block => {
                const display   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__display');
                const editor    = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__editor');
                const input     = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__input');
                const saveBtn   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__save');
                const cancelBtn = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__cancel');
                const errorEl   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__error');
                const field     = block.dataset.field;

                if (!display || !editor || !input) return;

                let originalValue = input.value;

                function openEditor() {
                    input.value = originalValue;
                    display.hidden = true;
                    editor.removeAttribute('hidden');
                    block.classList.add('sp-inline--editing');
                    input.focus();
                    if (input.tagName === 'INPUT')
                        input.setSelectionRange(input.value.length, input.value.length);
                }
                function closeEditor(restore) {
                    if (restore) input.value = originalValue;
                    display.hidden = false;
                    editor.setAttribute('hidden', '');
                    errorEl.hidden = true;
                    block.classList.remove('sp-inline--editing');
                }

                display.addEventListener('click', openEditor);
                cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => closeEditor(true));

                input.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
                    if (e.key === 'Escape') { e.preventDefault(); closeEditor(true); }
                    if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key === 'Enter') saveBtn.click();
                });

                saveBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                    const val = input.value.trim();
                    errorEl.hidden      = true;
                    saveBtn.disabled    = true;
                    saveBtn.textContent = 'Saving…';

                    const res = await saveTextField(field, val);

                    saveBtn.disabled    = false;
                    saveBtn.textContent = 'Save';

                    if (!res.ok) {
                        errorEl.textContent = res.error;
                        errorEl.hidden      = false;
                        return;
                    }

                    originalValue = val;

                    if (field === 'ShopName') {
                        // Update the text node inside the <h1> without clobbering the hint icon
                        const h1 = display;
                        const editHint = h1.querySelector('.sp-inline__edit-hint');
                        if (editHint) {
                            h1.childNodes[0].textContent = val + ' ';
                        } else {
                            h1.textContent = val;
                        }
                        document.title = val;
                    } else {
                        display.textContent = val || 'Click to add a bio…';
                        display.classList.toggle('sp-identity__bio--empty', !val);
                        if (val) {
                            // Re-append the hint icon for bio
                            const hint = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__edit-hint');
                            if (hint) display.appendChild(hint);
                        }
                    }

                    closeEditor(false);
                });
            });

        }());
    </script>
}

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var input   = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var form    = document.getElementById('addFundsForm');
            var btn     = document.getElementById('addFundsBtn');
            var presets = document.querySelectorAll('.addfunds-quick__btn');

            presets.forEach(function (p) {
                p.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    if (!input) return;
                    input.value = p.dataset.amount;
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    p.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                });
            });

            if (input) {
                input.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    presets.forEach(function (b) {
                        if (b.dataset.amount === input.value) b.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                    });
                });
            }

            if (form && btn) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.textContent = 'Processing…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}

    ViewData["Title"] = "My Wallet";

}

<div class="wlt-shell">

    @* ── Page header ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
    <header class="wlt-header">
        <div>
            <h1 class="wlt-header__title">My Wallet</h1>
            <p class="wlt-header__subtitle">Manage your balance and track every transaction.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="wlt-header__actions">
            <a asp-action="AddFunds" class="btn btn--primary">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">

                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
            </svg>

        </div>
    }
    @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
    {

            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-8-5a.75.75 0 01.75.75v4.5a.75.75 0 01-1.5 0v-4.5A.75.75 0 0110 5zm0 10a1 1 0 100-2 1 1 0 000 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
            </svg>
            @errMsg
        </div>
    }

    @* ── Balance cards ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
    <div class="wlt-cards">

        <div class="wlt-card wlt-card--available">
            <div class="wlt-card__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5">
                    <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M2.25 18.75a60.07 60.07 0 0115.797 2.101c.727.198 1.453-.342 1.453-1.096V18.75M3.75 4.5v.75A.75.75 0 013 6h-.75m0 0v-.375c0-.621.504-1.125 1.125-1.125H20.25M2.25 6v9m18-10.5v.75c0 .414.336.75.75.75h.75m-1.5-1.5h.375c.621 0 1.125.504 1.125 1.125v9.75c0 .621-.504 1.125-1.125 1.125h-.375m1.5-1.5H21a.75.75 0 00-.75.75v.75m0 0H3.75m0 0h-.375a1.125 1.125 0 01-1.125-1.125V15m1.5 1.5v-.75A.75.75 0 003 15h-.75M15 10.5a3 3 0 11-6 0 3 3 0 016 0zm3 0h.008v.008H18V10.5zm-12 0h.008v.008H6V10.5z" />
                </svg>
            </div>
            <div class="wlt-card__body">
                <p class="wlt-card__label">Available Balance</p>
                <p class="wlt-card__amount">₱@Model.Balance.ToString("N2")</p>
                <p class="wlt-card__hint">Ready to spend or withdraw</p>

                </svg>

        @* ── Transaction history ──────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <section class="wlt-section" aria-label="Transaction history">
            <header class="wlt-section__header">
                <h2 class="wlt-section__title">Transaction History</h2>
                <span class="wlt-section__count">Last @Model.RecentTransactions.Count</span>
            </header>

            @if (!Model.RecentTransactions.Any())
            {
                <div class="wlt-empty">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.3" aria-hidden="true">
                        <rect x="6" y="10" width="36" height="28" rx="4" />

                    </svg>
                    <p>No transactions yet.</p>
                </div>
            }
            else
            {
                <div class="wlt-tx-list">
                    @foreach (var tx in Model.RecentTransactions)
                    {
                        bool isCredit = tx.ToUserId == Model.CurrentUserId
                        && tx.Type != TransactionType.EscrowHold
                        && tx.Type != TransactionType.Withdrawal;
                        bool isDebit = !isCredit;

                        string typeLabel = tx.Type switch
                        {
                            TransactionType.EscrowHold => "Escrow Hold",
                            TransactionType.EscrowRelease => "Escrow Release",
                            TransactionType.Withdrawal => "Withdrawal",
                            TransactionType.CashCollection => "Cash Collected",
                            TransactionType.TopUp => "Funds Added",
                            _ => tx.Type.ToString()
                        };

                        string typeIcon = tx.Type switch
                        {
                            TransactionType.EscrowHold => "lock",
                            TransactionType.EscrowRelease => "unlock",
                            TransactionType.Withdrawal => "arrow-up",
                            TransactionType.CashCollection => "cash",
                            TransactionType.TopUp => "plus",
                            _ => "dot"
                        };

                        <div class="wlt-tx @(isCredit ? "wlt-tx--credit" : "wlt-tx--debit")">
                            <div class="wlt-tx__icon wlt-tx__icon--@typeIcon" aria-hidden="true">
                                @if (typeIcon == "lock")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 1a4.5 4.5 0 00-4.5 4.5V9H5a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2h-.5V5.5A4.5 4.5 0 0010 1zm3 8V5.5a3 3 0 10-6 0V9h6z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "unlock")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M14.5 1A4.5 4.5 0 0010 5.5V9H3a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2h-1.5V5.5a3 3 0 116 0v2.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0V5.5A4.5 4.5 0 0014.5 1z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "arrow-up")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 17a.75.75 0 01-.75-.75V5.612L5.29 9.77a.75.75 0 01-1.08-1.04l5.25-5.5a.75.75 0 011.08 0l5.25 5.5a.75.75 0 11-1.08 1.04l-3.96-4.158V16.25A.75.75 0 0110 17z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "cash")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path d="M10.75 10.818v2.614A3.13 3.13 0 0011.888 13c.482-.315.612-.648.612-.875 0-.227-.13-.56-.612-.875a3.13 3.13 0 00-1.138-.432zM8.33 8.62c.053.055.115.11.184.164.208.16.46.284.736.363V6.603a2.45 2.45 0 00-.35.13c-.14.065-.27.143-.386.233-.377.292-.514.627-.514.909 0 .184.058.39.33.585z" /><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 4a1 1 0 011-1h16a1 1 0 011 1v8a1 1 0 01-1 1H2a1 1 0 01-1-1V4zm2 3a2 2 0 00-2 2v1a2 2 0 002 2h.01A5.002 5.002 0 009.99 13H10a5 5 0 004.99-4.5H15a2 2 0 002-2V7a2 2 0 00-2-2v-.5a.5.5 0 00-1 0V5H6v-.5a.5.5 0 00-1 0V5H3z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                            </div>

                            <div class="wlt-tx__body">
                                <p class="wlt-tx__type">@typeLabel</p>
                                @if (tx.Order?.Item is not null)
                                {
                                    <p class="wlt-tx__ref">@tx.Order.Item.Title</p>
                                }
                                <p class="wlt-tx__date">
                                    <time datetime="@tx.CreatedAt.ToString("O")">
                                        @tx.CreatedAt.ToString("MMM d, yyyy · h:mm tt") UTC
                                    </time>
                                </p>
                            </div>

                            <div class="wlt-tx__amount @(isCredit ? "wlt-tx__amount--credit" : "wlt-tx__amount--debit")">
                                @(isCredit ? "+" : "−")₱@tx.Amount.ToString("N2")
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    }
                </div>
            }
        </section>

        @* ── Withdrawal history ───────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <section class="wlt-section" aria-label="Withdrawal requests">
            <header class="wlt-section__header">
                <h2 class="wlt-section__title">Withdrawals</h2>
                <a asp-action="Withdraw" class="wlt-section__cta">Request payout →</a>
            </header>

            @if (!Model.Withdrawals.Any())
            {
                <div class="wlt-empty">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.3" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path d="M24 10v28M14 20l10-10 10 10" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />

                    <p>No withdrawals yet.</p>
                </div>
            }
            else
            {
                <div class="wlt-wd-list">
                    @foreach (var wd in Model.Withdrawals)

                        string wdStatusClass = wd.Status switch
                        {

                            WithdrawalStatus.Processed => "wlt-badge--info",
                            WithdrawalStatus.Completed => "wlt-badge--success",
                            _ => ""
                        };

                        string wdMethodLabel = wd.Method switch
                        {
                            WithdrawalMethod.BankTransfer => "Bank Transfer",
                            WithdrawalMethod.PickupLocation => "Pickup",
                            _ => wd.Method.ToString()
                        };

                        <div class="wlt-wd">
                            <div class="wlt-wd__body">
                                <p class="wlt-wd__method">@wdMethodLabel</p>
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(wd.Reference))

                                }
                                <p class="wlt-wd__date">

                                        @wd.RequestedAt.ToString("MMM d, yyyy")
                                    </time>
                                </p>
                            </div>
                            <div class="wlt-wd__right">
                                <p class="wlt-wd__amount">₱@wd.Amount.ToString("N2")</p>
                                <span class="wlt-badge @wdStatusClass">@wd.Status</span>

                        </div>
                    }
                </div>
            }
        </section>

    </div>

</div>

@model ThriftLoop.ViewModels.WithdrawViewModel
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Withdraw Funds";
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
    decimal available = (decimal)(ViewBag.AvailableBalance ?? 0m);
}

<div class="wd-shell">

    <nav class="detail-breadcrumb" aria-label="Breadcrumb">

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var amountInput = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var allBtn      = document.getElementById('withdrawAllBtn');
            var wdForm      = document.getElementById('wdForm');
            var wdSubmitBtn = document.getElementById('wdSubmitBtn');
            var methodRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-radio');
            var methodLabels = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-option');

            // "Withdraw all" shortcut
            if (allBtn && amountInput) {
                allBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    amountInput.value = amountInput.max;
                });
            }

            // Sync method option visual state with radio selection
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio, i) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    methodLabels.forEach(function (lbl) { lbl.classList.remove('wd-method-option--active'); });
                    if (radio.checked) methodLabels[i].classList.add('wd-method-option--active');
                });
            });

            // Update reference hint based on method
            var referenceHint = document.getElementById('referenceHint');
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    if (!referenceHint) return;
                    referenceHint.textContent = radio.value === '1'
                        ? 'Your preferred pickup location or reference code.'
                        : 'Your bank account number or preferred pickup reference.';
                });
            });

            // Disable submit while in-flight
            if (wdForm && wdSubmitBtn) {
                wdForm.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    wdSubmitBtn.disabled = true;
                    wdSubmitBtn.textContent = 'Submitting…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}
